b699
(
	/ %YFramework $=
	(
		/ %YCLib $=
		(
			/ %FileSystem $=
			(
				/ @ !"platforms %(DS, Windows)" @ "function %ReadLink" $=
				(
					/ DLI "avoided redundant copy of result",
					/ "threw %std::invalid_argument for existed file which is \
						not a link"
						// This matches the behavior on platform %Win32
				),
				/ @ "platform %DS" @ "all functions %(ReadLink, \
					CreateHardLink, CreateSymbolicLink)" $=
				(
					+ $lib 'YB_NORETURN',
					(
					* "wrongly threw %std::system_error with \
						%std::errc::not_supported for 'char' overloads"
						~ "with %std::errc::function_not_supported" $since b652;
					* DD "wrong exception condition" @ "Doxygen command \
						'\exception'" @ "'char' overloads" $since b660
					),
					/ $design "assertion" ^ "%YAssertNonnull" ~ "%Nonnull"
				),
				+ "2 functions %ResolvePath",
				* "missing 'platform::'" @ "call of %FindColon" @ "function \
					templates %(IsAbsolute_P, FetchRootNameLength_P) with \
					%IDTag<YF_Platform_DS> parameter" $since b654,
				/ "constructor %DirectorySession" -> "default constructor and \
					2 explicit constructors with different string types and \
					'YB_NONNULL'",
					// To allow optimal initialization.
				/ "class %HDirectory" $=
				(
					/ DLDI "private data member"
						^ "brace-or-equal-initializer ' = 0'";
					/ "constructor %HDirectory"
						-> 'using DirectorySession::DirectorySession;'
				)
			),
			/ %FileIO $=
			(
				(
				/ "function %u16getcwd_n" -> "2 functions %ugetcwd with \
					overloading for both UTF-8 and UCS-2 buffer" $=
				(
					/ 'ynothrow' -> 'ynothrowv';
					+ "assertion to ensure nonnull parameter";
					* $comp "invalid 'YB_NONNULL'" $orig
						(@ %FileSystem $since b592)
						// The documents explicitly allowed null parameter.
				);
				+ "function template %TryGetCurrentWorkingDirectory" ^ $dep_from
					("%retry_for_vector" @ %YBase.YStandardEx.Container)
				)
				* $doc "wrong Doxygen command '\param'"
					@ "function %upclose" $orig (@ %FileSystem $since b566)
			)
		),
		/ %YSLib
		(
			/ $forced DLD 'using platform::u16getcwd_n;'
				-> 'using platform::ugetcwd' @ %Adaptor.YAdaptor $dep_from
				%YCLib.FileIO,
			/ %Service.FileSystem $=
			(
				/ $forced DLDI "function %FetchCurrentWorkingDirectory"
					$dep_from %Adaptor.YAdaptor,
				/ @ "functions %VerifyDirectory" $=
				(
					// To utilize optimal %DirectorySession constructors, esp. \
						on platform %Win32.
					+ "overloads of %VerifyDirectory for \
						('const char16_t*'; 'const u16string&')";
					/ DLP "optimized overloading for 'const String&'" ^ "%c_str"
						~ "%GetMBCS";
					/ $comp "optimized overloading for 'const Path&'"
				)
			)
		),
		/ DLDI "simplified %FetchModuleFileName" @ %'YCLib_(Win32)'.MinGW32
			^ $dep_from ("%retry_for_vector" @ %YBase.YStandardEx.Container)
	),
	+ "function template %retry_for_vector" @ %YBase.YStandardEx.Container
		// This is concerned with LWG 2466 but not a big issue in general. It \
			throws when allocation failed. It is user's responsibility to keep \
			it usable.
),

b697
(
	/ %YFramework $=
	(
		- "exception-specification" @ "destructor %JNIBase" %YCLib.JNI,
		/ %NPL.NPLA1 $=
		(
			/ DLI "improved performance"
				@ "functions %(RegisterContextHandler, \
				RegisterLiteralHandler)" ^ "%std::move",
			/ "constructor template" @ "classes %(FormContextHandler, \
				FunctionContextHandler)" ^ "forwarding reference parameter",
			+ "function template %ToContextHandler",
			/ @ "function template %RegisterFunction" $=
			(
				/ "forwarding reference parameter",
				/ DLDI "simplified" $dep_from "%ToContextHandler",
				/ $forced DLDI $dep_from "%RegisterContextHandler" ^ 'NPL::'
					~ 'A1::'
			),
			/ "supportted empty node" @ "function %ReduceFirst"
				~ "undefined behavior",
				// Even if for %Reduce it is guaranteed the parameter in first \
					iteration of list evaluation would not be an empty list \
					term, it is necessary for others. This is different to \
					%RemoveHead which has no sense for an empty node.
			+ "function %EvaluateContextFirst"
			/ "threw %ListEvaluationFailure if terms are not greater than 1"
				@ "member function %FunctionContextHandler::operator()",
			(
			+ "function %ReduceChildren";
			+ "2 inline overloaded functions %ReduceChildren",
			/ DLDI "simplified function %ReduceArguments" ^ "%ReduceChildren"
			),
			(
			/ "function %(TransformForSeperator, \
				TransformForSeperatorRecursive, ReplaceTermForSeperator)"
				=> "%(TransformForSeparator, TransformForSeparatorRecursive, \
				ReplaceSeparatedChildren)";
			* $comp "spelling error" $since b696,
			* "name not reserved if transformation occurred"
				@ "function %ReplaceSeparatedChildren"
				$orig (@ "function %ReplaceTermForSeperator" $since b696)
			);
			/ ("aliases %(ContextNode, ContextHandler, LiteralHandler), \
				'using YSLib::AccessChildPtr', functions \
				%(RegisterContextHandler, RegisterLiteralHandler, FetchValue, \
				LookupName, DetectReducible, LiftTerm, LiftFirst, LiftLast), \
				(class %PassCombinator; alias template %GPasses; aliases \
				%(TermPasses, EvaluationPasses)), aliases %(Guard; \
				GuardPasses), function template %InvokePasses"
				@ "namespace %A1") >> ("namespace %NPL" @ %NPLA)
				// Since %ValueNode has already been used in NPLA, many \
					algorithms should also be there.
		),
		* "unexpected ADL of %PostMessage call" @ "function template %PostTask"
			@ %YSLib.Core.Task $orig (@ %Helper.ShellHelper $since b448)
	),
	/ %YReader $=
	(
		- $revert(b534) "test for class %TreeView" @ "constructor %ShlExplorer"
			@ %ShlExplorer,
			// It has been effectively replaced by system information UI in \
				the "About" dialog.
		/ "made height of tree view 1pt less" @ "constructor \
			%SystemInformationPanel" @ %About
			// To avoid the border of the tree view touches the border of \
				buttons.
	)
),

(
	/ %YBase $=

			^ '__PRETTY_FUNCTION__',

		/ %YStandardEx $=
		(
			/ %TypeTraits $=
			(
				+ "unary type trait %is_referenceable",
				/ "binary type traits %(is_swappable_with, \
					is_nothrow_swappable_with)" $=
				(
					* "wrongly implied for lvalue reference type as parameters"
						$since b686,
					* "missing referenceable type check" $since b686
						$= (/ $impl ^ $dep_from "%is_referenceable")
				)
			),
			* "ill-formed use of 'size_type'" @ "function template %str_rfind#2"
				@ %CString $since b640
		)
	),
	/ %YFramework $=
	(
		/ %YSLib $=
		(
			/ %Service $=
			(
				/ "public data members %(nTextSize, nBlock, mBuffer)" @ "class \
					%TextFileBuffer" @ %TextManager -> "private data members",
					// It is dangerous to make them public. This also make \
						names conforming to convention about access-specifiers.
				/ %TextFile $=
				(
					/ $dev $lib "declarations of %(CheckBOM, DetectBOM) with \
						pointer parameters" ^ 'YB_NONNULL',
					+ "function %DetectBOM with %string_view parameter",
					/ @ "function %DetectBOM with 'istream&' parameter" $=
					(
						(
						/ "checked nonnegative read count result"
							^ "%(istream::gount, CheckNonnegativeScalar)",
						/ "tested BOM" ^ "%string_view" $dep_from
							"function %DetectBOM with %string_view parameter"
						);
						* $comp "non-empty BOM less than 4 bytes (that is, one \
							of UTF-8, UTF-16LE or UTF-16BE) not detected when \
							for files whose size is not greater than 4" $since
							b621,
					),
					* "wrongly detected UTF-16LE for UTF-32LE BOM"
						@ "functions %DetectBOM" $orig (@ "member function \
						%TextFile::CheckBOM" $since $before b132)
						// The order makes sense. Since UTF-16LE BOM is the \
							prefix of UTF-32LE BOM, it should be checked later.
				),
				* $comp "assertion failed for files with only a non-empty BOM \
					less than 4 bytes" @ "member function \
					%TextManager::operator[]" @ %TextManager $since b621
					$dep_from "%DecetBOM" @ %TextFile;
			),
			/ @ "class %TreeList" @ %UI.TreeView $=
			(
				* $doc "missing requirement on %ExtractText" $since b532,
				/ DLDI "function %GetIndentWidth" ^ "%IndentMap::cend"
					~ "%IndentMap::end",
				/ @ "function %Bind" $=
				(
					* "missing strong exception safety" $since b532;
					* $comp "corrupted contents by duplicate calls due to \
						missing clearing list, indent map and expanded set"
						$since b532
				),
				* "invalid access at end of indent map"
					@ "function %CheckNodeState" $since b532
			)
		),
		(
		+ "function %FetchModuleFileName" @ %'YCLib_(Win32)'.MinGW32;
		/ "adjusted default base path for root of configuartion and \
			configuration file path based on image base path" @ "platform \
			%Win32" @ %Helper.Initialization ~ "current working directory"
		)
	),
	/ %YReader $=
	(
		* $comp "assertion failed for files with only a non-empty BOM less \
			than 4 bytes" @ %DSReader $since b621 $dep_from
			%YFramework.YSLib.Service.TextManager,
			// This would cause inifinte loop with identical conversion states \
				for specific files after the assertion is suppressed.
		* $comp "crash after collapse and expanding at last node" @ "tree view \
			test" @ %ShlExplorer $since b534 $dep_from
			("%TreeList::CheckNodeState" @ %YFramework.YSLib.UI.TreeView)

b692
(
	/ %YFramework $=
	(
		/ %NPL.NPLA $=
		(
			+ "class %ListReductionFailure",
			/ "rethrew %NPLException on catching at first"
				@ "member function %FormContextHandler::operator()" @ %NPLA1
		),
		/ @ "namespace %Concurrency" @ %YCLib.Mutex $dep_from
			%YBase.YStandardEx.PseudoMutex $=
		(
			+ 'using YCL_Mutex_Namespace::once_flag;',
			+ 'using YCL_Mutex_Namespace::call_once;'
		),
		/ DLI "initialization of host and environment before application \
			internal instance pointer initialization" @ "class GUIApplication"
			@ %Helper.GUIApplication
			^ ("%ystdex::call_once_init", "%once_flag" $dep_from %YCLib.Mutex)
	),
	/ %YBase.YStandardEx $=
	(
		+ "struct %once_flag" @ "namespace %single_thread" @ %PseudoMutex,
		/ "function template %call_once for 'bool'" -> ("function template for \
			%once_flag" @ "namespace %single_thread" @ %PseudoMutex) $dep_from
			%PseudoMutex,
		/ @ "class template %state_guard" %ScopeGuard $=
		(
			/ DLDI "simplified" ^ "%noncopyable",
			- "data member %data" @ "all specializations",
				// It is dangerous to leave different types as union members.
			/ ("mutable data member %enabled" -> "function %engaged")
				@ "non %void condition type specialization",
			(
			/ DLDI "simplified" ^ $dep_from
				("%ystdex::(construct_in, destroy_in)" @ %Memory);
			* $comp "missing '::' before placement 'new' expression for \
				construction" $since b525 $orig (@ %Utilities)
			)
		),
		/ %Any $=
		(
			+ DLDI 'muatble' @ "any storage" @ "class %any" $dep_to
				"mutable any storage";
			/ "all 'const any_stroage&' parameter type" @ "manager"
				-> 'any_storage&' $effective @ ("alias %any_manager",
				"all static functions %manage" @ "class templates \
				%(value_handler, ref_handler)", "static functions \
				%(get_reference, get_pointer)" @ "class template %ref_handler",
				"static functions %(get_holder_pointer, get_pointer)"
				@ "class template %holder_handler" @ "namespace %any_ops");
			/ $forced "split for const qualifier" @ "functions %(get_pointer, \
				get_reference)" @ "class template %value_handler",
			/ $forced DLDI ("function %call" !^ "%get_reference")

					list of %Tokenize result for null-terminated character \

					NPL units"

				/ DLDI "simplified function %Literalize"
			),
			/ "function %operator for %File and %Configuration" @ %Configuration
				-> "function %operator<< for %std::ostream and %Configuration"
				$dep_from %YSLib.Service.File,
			/ %NPLA1 $=
			(
				/ DLDI "function template% InsertChildSyntaxNode#3"
					^ "%TransformToSyntaxNode" ~ "%NodeLiteral::GetSyntaxNode",

					>> ("namespace %NPL" @ %NPL.Configuration)

		),
		* $dev $build $impl "wrong returned value cast of %::ShllExecuteW"
			@ "function %ExecuteShellCommand" @ "platform %Win32"
